The connection manager bases further\n36:  * filter invocations on the return code of the previous filter.\n37:  */\n38: enum class FilterHeadersStatus {\n39:   // Continue filter chain iteration.\n40:   Continue,\n41:   // Do not iterate for headers on any of the remaining filters in the chain.\n42:   //\n43:   // Returning FilterDataStatus::Continue from decodeData()/encodeData() or calling\n44:   // continueDecoding()/continueEncoding() MUST be called if continued filter iteration is desired.\n45:   //\n46:   // Note that if a local reply was sent, no further iteration for headers as well as data and\n47:   // trailers for the current filter and the filters following will happen. A local reply can be\n48:   // triggered via sendLocalReply() or encodeHeaders().\n49:   StopIteration,\n50:   // Continue headers iteration to remaining filters, but delay ending the stream. This status MUST\n51:   // NOT be returned when end_stream is already set to false.\n52:   //\n53:   // Used when a filter wants to add a body to a headers-only request/response, but this body is not\n54:   // readily available. Delaying end_stream allows the filter to add the body once it's available\n55:   // without stopping headers iteration.\n56:   //\n57:   // The filter is responsible to continue the stream by providing a body through calling\n58:   // injectDecodedDataToFilterChain()/injectEncodedDataToFilterChain(), possibly multiple times\n59:   // if the body needs to be divided into several chunks. The filter may need to handle\n60:   // watermark events when injecting a body, see:\n61:   // https://github.com/envoyproxy/envoy/blob/main/source/docs/flow_control.md.\n62:   //\n63:   // The last call to inject data MUST have end_stream set to true to conclude the stream.\n64:   // If the filter cannot provide a body the stream should be reset.\n65:   //\n66:   // Adding a body through calling addDecodedData()/addEncodedData() then\n67:   // continueDecoding()/continueEncoding() is currently NOT supported and causes an assert failure.\n68:   //\n69:   // Adding trailers in this scenario is currently NOT supported.\n70:   //\n71:   // The filter MUST NOT attempt to continue the stream without providing a body using\n72:   // continueDecoding()/continueEncoding().\n73:   //\n74:   // TODO(yosrym93): Support adding a body in this case by calling addDecodedData()/addEncodedData()\n75:   // then continueDecoding()/continueEncoding(). separates interface definitions from implementations across several key components:\\n\\n## 1. Core Interfaces (envoy/http/filter_factory.h)\\nDefines the fundamental abstractions:\\n- **FilterFactoryCb**: A function type that wraps filter creation (`std::function<void(FilterChainFactoryCallbacks&)>`). This is the callback invoked at runtime to instantiate filters.\\n- **FilterContext**: A struct containing metadata about a filter (config_name and filter_name) passed during filter chain creation.\\n- **FilterChainManager**: Interface that connection managers implement to receive and apply filter factories. The key method is `applyFilterFactoryCb()` which accepts a FilterContext and FilterFactoryCb.\\n- **FilterChainFactory**: Interface for creating HTTP filter chains when new streams are created.\\n\\n## 2. Filter Base Classes (envoy/http/filter.h)\\nDefines the filter types that can be registered:\\n- **StreamFilterBase**: Base class for all HTTP filters with lifecycle management (onDestroy, onStreamComplete).\\n- **StreamDecoderFilter**: Processes request headers, data, and trailers flowing downstream.\\n- **StreamEncoderFilter**: Processes response headers, data, and trailers flowing upstream.\\n- **FilterChainFactoryCallbacks**: Interface used by filters to register themselves in a chain (addStreamDecoderFilter, addStreamEncoderFilter, addStreamFilter).\\n\\n## 3. Filter Factory Registry (envoy/server/filter_config.h)\\nDefines the factory interfaces for registration:\\n- **HttpFilterConfigFactoryBase**: Base class for all HTTP filter factories with methods to create empty config protos and route-specific configs.\\n- **NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory**: Interface that filter implementations register with to create downstream HTTP filters. Method `createFilterFactoryFromProto()` returns FilterFactoryCb.\\n- **UpstreamHttpFilterConfigFactory**: Similar to NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory but for upstream (to-cluster) filters.\\n\\n## 4. Template Factory Base (source/extensions/filters/http/common/factory_base.h)\\nProvides boilerplate reduction:\\n- **CommonFactoryBase**: Template base with protobuf message handling and route config support.\\n- **FactoryBase**: Inherits from CommonFactoryBase and NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory, implementing createFilterFactoryFromProto() that calls the pure virtual createFilterFactoryFromProtoTyped().\\n- **DualFactoryBase**: Supports both downstream and upstream by inheriting from both NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory and UpstreamHttpFilterConfigFactory.\\n\\n## 5. Per-Request Filter Chain Execution (source/common/http/filter_manager.h and filter_manager.cc)\\nManages the actual runtime filter chain for each stream:\\n- **FilterManager**: Main class managing filter chains for a connection. Contains the stream state, filters lists, and iteration logic.\\n- **ActiveStreamFilterBase**: Wrapper around each filter instance tracking:\\n  - Iteration state (Continue, StopIteration, etc.)\\n  - Whether it's encoder or decoder (or both)\\n  - FilterContext metadata\\n  - Methods like commonContinue() to resume iteration after async operations\\n- **FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl**: Implementation of FilterChainFactoryCallbacks that adds decoded/encoded/stream filters to the FilterManager's lists.\\n- The execution chain is a bidirectional list of ActiveStreamDecoderFilter and ActiveStreamEncoderFilter objects that are iterated through.\\n\\n## 6. Dynamic Filter Discovery (source/common/filter/config_discovery_impl.h and config_discovery_impl.cc)\\nEnables ECDS (Extension Config Discovery Service) for dynamic filter loading:\\n- **NamedHttpFilterFactoryCb**: Struct combining filter name and FilterFactoryCb (line 185-190).\\n- **DynamicFilterConfigProviderImpl**: Template class managing filter discovery subscriptions, handling configuration updates and thread-local storage of filter factories.\\n- **HttpDynamicFilterConfigProviderImpl**: Specialization for HTTP filters that instantiates filter factories from discovered configurations by calling the appropriate NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory.\\n\\n## 7. Filter Chain Construction (source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h and filter_chain_helper.cc)\\nOrchestrates filter chain assembly from configuration:\\n- **FilterChainUtility**: Static methods for:\\n  - createFilterChainForFactories(): Iterates through FilterFactoriesList and calls applyFilterFactoryCb for each.\\n  - Singleton factory management for downstream/upstream filter config providers.\\n- **FilterChainHelper**: Template class that processes filter configuration protos to build FilterFactoriesList, handling both static and dynamic (ECDS) filters. The processFilters() method validates dependencies and creates filter config providers.\\n\\n## 8. Filter Manager Implementation (source/common/listener_manager/filter_chain_manager_impl.h and filter_chain_manager_impl.cc)\\nImplements FilterChainManager interface:\\n- **FilterChainManagerImpl**: Manages network-level filter chains with support for hot reloading and multi-address listeners.\\n\\n## Execution Flow:\\n1. **Configuration Time**: FilterChainHelper processes HttpFilter protos, looking up NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory for each filter, calling createFilterFactoryFromProto() to get FilterFactoryCb, and storing in FilterFactoriesList.\\n2. **Stream Creation**: When a new HTTP stream is created, FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories() iterates the list and calls FilterChainManager::applyFilterFactoryCb().\\n3. **Filter Instantiation**: applyFilterFactoryCb() creates FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl and invokes the FilterFactoryCb, which calls addStreamDecoderFilter/addStreamEncoderFilter/addStreamFilter on the callbacks.\\n4. **Filter Execution**: FilterManager maintains lists of ActiveStreamDecoderFilter and ActiveStreamEncoderFilter, iterating through them as data flows (headers, data, trailers) bidirectionally. The commonContinue() methods in ActiveStreamFilterBase handle resumption after filters return StopIteration or async operations complete.\\n5. **Dynamic Updates**: HttpDynamicFilterConfigProviderImpl listens for ECDS updates, instantiates new filter factories on config change, and updates thread-local storage atomically across worker threads.\\n\\nThe architecture separates concerns cleanly: interface definitions (filter.h, filter_factory.h) from factory registration (filter_config.h), template helpers (factory_base.h), and runtime execution (filter_manager.h/cc).\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":5240,"cache_read_input_tokens":105298,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":5240},"output_tokens":4,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"c1e6a8c5-2d56-48ca-b29e-31cb91681a58","uuid":"2545b6b5-b79f-4b73-9aef-d286c1d1841e"}

separates interface definitions from implementations across several key components:\\n\\n## 1. Core Interfaces (envoy/http/filter_factory.h)\\nDefines the fundamental abstractions:\\n- **FilterFactoryCb**: A function type that wraps filter creation (`std::function<void(FilterChainFactoryCallbacks&)>`). This is the callback invoked at runtime to instantiate filters.\\n- **FilterContext**: A struct containing metadata about a filter (config_name and filter_name) passed during filter chain creation.\\n- **FilterChainManager**: Interface that connection managers implement to receive and apply filter factories. The key method is `applyFilterFactoryCb()` which accepts a FilterContext and FilterFactoryCb.\\n- **FilterChainFactory**: Interface for creating HTTP filter chains when new streams are created.\\n\\n## 2. Filter Base Classes (envoy/http/filter.h)\\nDefines the filter types that can be registered:\\n- **StreamFilterBase**: Base class for all HTTP filters with lifecycle management (onDestroy, onStreamComplete).\\n- **StreamDecoderFilter**: Processes request headers, data, and trailers flowing downstream.\\n- **StreamEncoderFilter**: Processes response headers, data, and trailers flowing upstream.\\n- **FilterChainFactoryCallbacks**: Interface used by filters to register themselves in a chain (addStreamDecoderFilter, addStreamEncoderFilter, addStreamFilter).\\n\\n## 3. Filter Factory Registry (envoy/server/filter_config.h)\\nDefines the factory interfaces for registration:\\n- **HttpFilterConfigFactoryBase**: Base class for all HTTP filter factories with methods to create empty config protos and route-specific configs.\\n- **NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory**: Interface that filter implementations register with to create downstream HTTP filters. Method `createFilterFactoryFromProto()` returns FilterFactoryCb.\\n- **UpstreamHttpFilterConfigFactory**: Similar to NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory but for upstream (to-cluster) filters.\\n\\n## 4. Template Factory Base (source/extensions/filters/http/common/factory_base.h)\\nProvides boilerplate reduction:\\n- **CommonFactoryBase**: Template base with protobuf message handling and route config support.\\n- **FactoryBase**: Inherits from CommonFactoryBase and NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory, implementing createFilterFactoryFromProto() that calls the pure virtual createFilterFactoryFromProtoTyped().\\n- **DualFactoryBase**: Supports both downstream and upstream by inheriting from both NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory and UpstreamHttpFilterConfigFactory.\\n\\n## 5. Per-Request Filter Chain Execution (source/common/http/filter_manager.h and filter_manager.cc)\\nManages the actual runtime filter chain for each stream:\\n- **FilterManager**: Main class managing filter chains for a connection. Contains the stream state, filters lists, and iteration logic.\\n- **ActiveStreamFilterBase**: Wrapper around each filter instance tracking:\\n  - Iteration state (Continue, StopIteration, etc.)\\n  - Whether it's encoder or decoder (or both)\\n  - FilterContext metadata\\n  - Methods like commonContinue() to resume iteration after async operations\\n- **FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl**: Implementation of FilterChainFactoryCallbacks that adds decoded/encoded/stream filters to the FilterManager's lists.\\n- The execution chain is a bidirectional list of ActiveStreamDecoderFilter and ActiveStreamEncoderFilter objects that are iterated through.\\n\\n## 6. Dynamic Filter Discovery (source/common/filter/config_discovery_impl.h and config_discovery_impl.cc)\\nEnables ECDS (Extension Config Discovery Service) for dynamic filter loading:\\n- **NamedHttpFilterFactoryCb**: Struct combining filter name and FilterFactoryCb (line 185-190).\\n- **DynamicFilterConfigProviderImpl**: Template class managing filter discovery subscriptions, handling configuration updates and thread-local storage of filter factories.\\n- **HttpDynamicFilterConfigProviderImpl**: Specialization for HTTP filters that instantiates filter factories from discovered configurations by calling the appropriate NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory.\\n\\n## 7. Filter Chain Construction (source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h and filter_chain_helper.cc)\\nOrchestrates filter chain assembly from configuration:\\n- **FilterChainUtility**: Static methods for:\\n  - createFilterChainForFactories(): Iterates through FilterFactoriesList and calls applyFilterFactoryCb for each.\\n  - Singleton factory management for downstream/upstream filter config providers.\\n- **FilterChainHelper**: Template class that processes filter configuration protos to build FilterFactoriesList, handling both static and dynamic (ECDS) filters. The processFilters() method validates dependencies and creates filter config providers.\\n\\n## 8. Filter Manager Implementation (source/common/listener_manager/filter_chain_manager_impl.h and filter_chain_manager_impl.cc)\\nImplements FilterChainManager interface:\\n- **FilterChainManagerImpl**: Manages network-level filter chains with support for hot reloading and multi-address listeners.\\n\\n## Execution Flow:\\n1. **Configuration Time**: FilterChainHelper processes HttpFilter protos, looking up NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory for each filter, calling createFilterFactoryFromProto() to get FilterFactoryCb, and storing in FilterFactoriesList.\\n2. **Stream Creation**: When a new HTTP stream is created, FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories() iterates the list and calls FilterChainManager::applyFilterFactoryCb().\\n3. **Filter Instantiation**: applyFilterFactoryCb() creates FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl and invokes the FilterFactoryCb, which calls addStreamDecoderFilter/addStreamEncoderFilter/addStreamFilter on the callbacks.\\n4. **Filter Execution**: FilterManager maintains lists of ActiveStreamDecoderFilter and ActiveStreamEncoderFilter, iterating through them as data flows (headers, data, trailers) bidirectionally. The commonContinue() methods in ActiveStreamFilterBase handle resumption after filters return StopIteration or async operations complete.\\n5. **Dynamic Updates**: HttpDynamicFilterConfigProviderImpl listens for ECDS updates, instantiates new filter factories on config change, and updates thread-local storage atomically across worker threads.\\n\\nThe architecture separates concerns cleanly: interface definitions (filter.h, filter_factory.h) from factory registration (filter_config.h), template helpers (factory_base.h), and runtime execution (filter_manager.h/cc).\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
